<script>
(function(){
  // ===== Tunables =====
  var SOCIAL_COOLDOWN_H = 3;     // Telegram/Facebook once per 6h
  var PAGE_COOLDOWN_MIN = 10;    // default page cooldown (minutes) applied ONLY after click
  var SOCIAL_WEIGHT_TG  = 40;    // % chance to prefer Telegram over Facebook

  // ===== Pools (from PHP) =====
  var isAdult   = false;
  var TELEGRAM  = "https:\/\/t.me\/+_3q-RJ0CIpA1OTZl";
  var FACEBOOK  = "https:\/\/www.facebook.com\/groups\/1334707517706527";
  var JAYA9     = ["https:\/\/www.jaya9bangladesh.com\/?af=AG000332","https:\/\/www.jaya9bangladesh.com\/?af=AG000332","https:\/\/www.jaya9bangladesh.com\/?af=AG000332"];
  var EXTRA     = ["https:\/\/rectangularfoundation.com\/bV3BV\/0DP.3dpnv\/b\/mcVfJBZ-D\/0\/1WNBj\/I-zPNpzRkF2ALsT-UX2uMAjqM\/3TOMTbcE"];
  var ADULT     = ["https:\/\/rectangularfoundation.com\/bV3BV\/0DP.3dpnv\/b\/mcVfJBZ-D\/0\/1WNBj\/I-zPNpzRkF2ALsT-UX2uMAjqM\/3TOMTbcE","https:\/\/rectangularfoundation.com\/bV3BV\/0DP.3dpnv\/b\/mcVfJBZ-D\/0\/1WNBj\/I-zPNpzRkF2ALsT-UX2uMAjqM\/3TOMTbcE","https:\/\/rectangularfoundation.com\/bV3BV\/0DP.3dpnv\/b\/mcVfJBZ-D\/0\/1WNBj\/I-zPNpzRkF2ALsT-UX2uMAjqM\/3TOMTbcE"];

  // ===== Helpers =====
  function isHuman(){
    var ua = (navigator.userAgent||'').toLowerCase();
    if (!ua) return false;
    if (/(bot|crawl|spider|slurp|curl|wget|httpclient)/i.test(ua)) return false;
    if (navigator.webdriver) return false;
    return true;
  }
  function inEditableArea(t){
    return !!(t && t.closest && t.closest('input, textarea, select, [contenteditable="true"], .search-container'));
  }
  function pickRandom(arr){
    if (!arr || !arr.length) return null;
    if (arr.length === 1) return arr[0];
    var r = Math.random();
    if (r < 0.6) return arr[0];
    if (r < 0.8) return arr[1 % arr.length];
    return arr[2 % arr.length];
  }
  function pickSocial(){
    return (Math.random()*100 < SOCIAL_WEIGHT_TG) ? TELEGRAM : FACEBOOK;
  }
  function setCookie(name, val, minutes){
    var expires = '';
    if (minutes && minutes > 0){
      var d = new Date();
      d.setTime(d.getTime() + minutes*60*1000);
      expires = '; expires='+ d.toUTCString();
    }
    document.cookie = name+'='+encodeURIComponent(val||'')+expires+'; path=/; SameSite=Lax';
  }
  function getCookie(name){
    var m = document.cookie.match(new RegExp('(^| )'+name+'=([^;]+)'));
    return m ? decodeURIComponent(m[2]) : null;
  }

  // IMPORTANT: do NOT set any page-level storage on load.

  if (!isHuman()) return;

  // Keys scoped per-URL (but created only after click)
  var urlKey = (location.pathname + location.search + location.hash) || 'root';
  try { urlKey = encodeURIComponent(urlKey); } catch(e){}
  var KEY_ONCE   = 'mlbd_once_'  + urlKey; // sessionStorage
  var KEY_TWICE  = 'mlbd_twice_' + urlKey; // sessionStorage
  var PAGE_CD    = 'mlbd_pg_cd_' + urlKey; // cookie (minutes)
  var SOCIAL_KEY = 'mlbd_social_cd';       // cookie (minutes)

  // Cooldown state (read-only on load; we won't write yet)
  var socialOK = !getCookie(SOCIAL_KEY);
  var pageOK   = !getCookie(PAGE_CD);

  // Choose links lazily (no writes)
  var firstLink = null, secondLink = null;
  if (pageOK){
    if (isAdult){
      if (socialOK){
        firstLink  = pickSocial();
        secondLink = pickRandom(ADULT);
      } else {
        firstLink  = pickRandom(ADULT);
        secondLink = pickRandom(ADULT);
      }
    } else {
      if (socialOK){
        firstLink  = pickSocial();
        secondLink = pickRandom(JAYA9);
      } else {
        firstLink  = pickRandom(JAYA9);
        secondLink = pickRandom(EXTRA);
      }
    }
  }
  var adsActive = !!firstLink;

  // Impression beacon ‚Äî fired ONLY when we actually open an ad
  function sendImp(pool, position){
    try{
      var payload = { pool: pool, position: position, ts: Date.now(), url: location.pathname };
      var blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(payload)], {type:'application/json'});
      navigator.sendBeacon('/imp.php', blob);
    }catch(e){}
  }

  function poolNameByLink(l){
    if (!l) return 'unknown';
    if (l === TELEGRAM) return 'social:telegram';
    if (l === FACEBOOK) return 'social:facebook';
    if (Array.isArray(JAYA9)  && JAYA9.indexOf(l)  !== -1) return 'jaya9';
    if (Array.isArray(EXTRA)  && EXTRA.indexOf(l)  !== -1) return 'extra';
    if (Array.isArray(ADULT)  && ADULT.indexOf(l)  !== -1) return 'adult';
    if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('t.me')         !== -1) return 'social:telegram';
    if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('facebook.com')  !== -1) return 'social:facebook';
    if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('jaya9')         !== -1) return 'jaya9';
    if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('understatedplace') !== -1) return 'extra';
    if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('neat-price')    !== -1) return 'adult';
    return 'unknown';
  }

  // ===== Protection setters ‚Äî ONLY after click =====
  function markSocialCooldown(){
    setCookie(SOCIAL_KEY, '1', SOCIAL_COOLDOWN_H*60); // minutes
  }
  function markPageCooldown(){
    // Optionally adjust by simple heuristics at click-time (not on load)
    var minutes = PAGE_COOLDOWN_MIN;
    var conn = (navigator.connection || {});
    if (/^(slow-2g|2g)$/.test(conn.effectiveType||'')) minutes += 5;
    if (isAdult) minutes = Math.max(8, minutes - 3);
    setCookie(PAGE_CD, '1', minutes);
  }

  // Track per-URL ‚Äúalready fired‚Äù in sessionStorage (but write only after click)
  var firedOnce  = false;
  var firedTwice = false;

  function handleClick(e){
    // Only real user clicks; ignore programmatic/synthetic events
    if (!e || !e.isTrusted) return;
    if (inEditableArea(e.target)) return;

    // First ad
    if (adsActive && !firedOnce && firstLink){
      firedOnce = true;
      try { sessionStorage.setItem(KEY_ONCE, '1'); } catch(_) {}
      sendImp(poolNameByLink(firstLink), 1);
      try { window.open(firstLink, '_blank', 'noopener'); } catch(_){}
      if (firstLink === TELEGRAM || firstLink === FACEBOOK) markSocialCooldown();
      // If no second to show later, start page cooldown now
      if (!secondLink) markPageCooldown();
      return;
    }

    // Second ad (if any)
    if (adsActive && !firedTwice && secondLink){
      firedTwice = true;
      try { sessionStorage.setItem(KEY_TWICE, '1'); } catch(_) {}
      sendImp(poolNameByLink(secondLink), 2);
      try { window.open(secondLink, '_blank', 'noopener'); } catch(_){}
      markPageCooldown();
      return;
    }
  }
  document.addEventListener('click', handleClick, true);

  // Optional helper to tie into your main CTA button
  window.showLoadingButton = function(button, primaryLink){
    // Behaves the same as a user click, and only then sets cooldowns
    if (adsActive && !firedOnce && firstLink){
      firedOnce = true;
      try { sessionStorage.setItem(KEY_ONCE, '1'); } catch(_) {}
      sendImp(poolNameByLink(firstLink), 1);
      try { window.open(firstLink, '_blank', 'noopener'); } catch(_){}
      if (firstLink === TELEGRAM || firstLink === FACEBOOK) markSocialCooldown();
      if (!secondLink) markPageCooldown();
    } else if (adsActive && !firedTwice && secondLink){
      firedTwice = true;
      try { sessionStorage.setItem(KEY_TWICE, '1'); } catch(_) {}
      sendImp(poolNameByLink(secondLink), 2);
      try { window.open(secondLink, '_blank', 'noopener'); } catch(_){}
      markPageCooldown();
    }
    if (primaryLink){
      setTimeout(function(){ window.location.assign(primaryLink); }, 0);
    }
  };
})();

    (function(){
        // Disable DevTools shortcut keys
        document.addEventListener("contextmenu", function(e) {
            const selection = window.getSelection().toString();
            const isInsideSearch = e.target.closest(".search-container");
            if (!selection && !isInsideSearch) e.preventDefault();
        });

        document.addEventListener("keydown", function(e) {
            const key = e.key.toUpperCase();
            const ctrl = e.ctrlKey, shift = e.shiftKey;
            const isSearch = document.activeElement?.closest(".search-container");
            const allow = isSearch && (key === "C" || key === "V");
            if (
                e.keyCode === 123 || 
                (ctrl && shift && ["I", "J"].includes(key)) ||
                (ctrl && key === "U") ||
                (!allow && ctrl && ["C", "V"].includes(key))
            ) {
                e.preventDefault();
            }
        });

        function showBlockMessage(title, message) {
            document.body.innerHTML = '';
            const div = document.createElement("div");
            div.style.cssText = "position:fixed;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;background:#000;color:#0f0;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-direction:column;font-size:18px;z-index:999999;text-align:center;padding:2rem";
            div.innerHTML = "<h2 style='font-size:2.5em'>" + title + "</h2><p>" + message + "</p>";
            document.body.appendChild(div);
        }

        let blocked = false;
        function detectDevTools() {
            const start = performance.now();
            debugger;
            return performance.now() - start > 100;
        }

        setInterval(() => {
            if (!blocked && detectDevTools()) {
                blocked = true;
                showBlockMessage("DevTools is open!", "Close DevTools and reload.");
            }
        }, 1500);

        // Bait detection
        let bait = "off";
        const img = new Image();
        Object.defineProperty(img, 'id', {
            get: function () {
                bait = "on";
                throw new Error("DevTools Detected");
            }
        });

        setInterval(() => {
            bait = "off";
            console.dir(img);
            if (bait === "on" && !blocked) {
                blocked = true;
                showBlockMessage("Chrome inspection blocked!", "Reload after closing DevTools.");
            }
        }, 2000);
    })();

    // === Filter Toggle Logic
    (function(){
        const onlyNewOn = false;
        const hide18On = true;

        function setCookie(name, value, days) {
            const expires = new Date(Date.now() + days * 86400000).toUTCString();
            document.cookie = name + '=' + value + '; expires=' + expires + '; path=/';
        }

        let newToggle = onlyNewOn;
        let adultToggle = hide18On;

        function filterCards() {
            document.querySelectorAll('.movie-card').forEach(card => {
                const is18 = card.dataset['18'] === '1';
                const isNew = card.dataset['new'] === '1';
                const img = card.querySelector('img');
                if (adultToggle && is18 && img) {
                    img.classList.add('blurred-card');
                } else if (img) {
                    img.classList.remove('blurred-card');
                }
                card.style.display = (!newToggle || isNew) ? 'block' : 'none';
            });
        }

        document.getElementById('toggleOnlyNew')?.addEventListener('click', function () {
            newToggle = !newToggle;
            setCookie('only_new', newToggle ? '1' : '0', 30);
            this.textContent = 'Only New: ' + (newToggle ? 'Yes' : 'No');
            this.classList.toggle('bg-green', newToggle);
            this.classList.toggle('bg-red', !newToggle);
            filterCards();
        });

        document.getElementById('toggle18Btn')?.addEventListener('click', function () {
            adultToggle = !adultToggle;
            setCookie('hide_18', adultToggle ? '1' : '0', 30);
            this.textContent = 'Hide 18+: ' + (adultToggle ? 'Yes' : 'No');
            this.classList.toggle('bg-green', adultToggle);
            this.classList.toggle('bg-red', !adultToggle);
            filterCards();
        });

        filterCards();
    })();
    </script>

        function toast(msg){
  const t=document.createElement('div');
  t.className='mlb-toast'; t.textContent=msg;
  document.body.appendChild(t);
  setTimeout(()=>{t.style.opacity='0';t.style.transition='opacity .25s';},1000);
  setTimeout(()=>t.remove(),1300);
}
function copyDirectLink(val){
  try{
    if(navigator.clipboard && window.isSecureContext){
      navigator.clipboard.writeText(val);
    }else{
      const ta=document.createElement("textarea");
      ta.value=val; ta.style.position="fixed"; ta.style.left="-9999px";
      document.body.appendChild(ta); ta.select(); document.execCommand("copy"); ta.remove();
    }
    toast("Link copied!");
  }catch(e){ toast("Copy failed"); }
}
</script>

  <script>
    (function() {
      // ===== Tunables =====
      var SOCIAL_COOLDOWN_H = 3; // Telegram/Facebook once per 6h
      var PAGE_COOLDOWN_MIN = 10; // default page cooldown (minutes) applied ONLY after click
      var SOCIAL_WEIGHT_TG = 40; // % chance to prefer Telegram over Facebook

      // ===== Pools (from PHP) =====
      var isAdult = false;
      var TELEGRAM = "https:\/\/t.me\/+_3q-RJ0CIpA1OTZl";
      var FACEBOOK = "https:\/\/www.facebook.com\/groups\/1334707517706527";
      var JAYA9 = ["https:\/\/www.jaya9bangladesh.com\/?af=AG000332", "https:\/\/www.jaya9bangladesh.com\/?af=AG000332", "https:\/\/www.jaya9bangladesh.com\/?af=AG000332"];
      var EXTRA = ["https:\/\/rectangularfoundation.com\/bV3BV\/0DP.3dpnv\/b\/mcVfJBZ-D\/0\/1WNBj\/I-zPNpzRkF2ALsT-UX2uMAjqM\/3TOMTbcE"];
      var ADULT = ["https:\/\/rectangularfoundation.com\/bV3BV\/0DP.3dpnv\/b\/mcVfJBZ-D\/0\/1WNBj\/I-zPNpzRkF2ALsT-UX2uMAjqM\/3TOMTbcE", "https:\/\/rectangularfoundation.com\/bV3BV\/0DP.3dpnv\/b\/mcVfJBZ-D\/0\/1WNBj\/I-zPNpzRkF2ALsT-UX2uMAjqM\/3TOMTbcE", "https:\/\/rectangularfoundation.com\/bV3BV\/0DP.3dpnv\/b\/mcVfJBZ-D\/0\/1WNBj\/I-zPNpzRkF2ALsT-UX2uMAjqM\/3TOMTbcE"];

      // ===== Helpers =====
      function isHuman() {
        var ua = (navigator.userAgent || '').toLowerCase();
        if (!ua) return false;
        if (/(bot|crawl|spider|slurp|curl|wget|httpclient)/i.test(ua)) return false;
        if (navigator.webdriver) return false;
        return true;
      }

      function inEditableArea(t) {
        return !!(t && t.closest && t.closest('input, textarea, select, [contenteditable="true"], .search-container'));
      }

      function pickRandom(arr) {
        if (!arr || !arr.length) return null;
        if (arr.length === 1) return arr[0];
        var r = Math.random();
        if (r < 0.6) return arr[0];
        if (r < 0.8) return arr[1 % arr.length];
        return arr[2 % arr.length];
      }

      function pickSocial() {
        return (Math.random() * 100 < SOCIAL_WEIGHT_TG) ? TELEGRAM : FACEBOOK;
      }

      function setCookie(name, val, minutes) {
        var expires = '';
        if (minutes && minutes > 0) {
          var d = new Date();
          d.setTime(d.getTime() + minutes * 60 * 1000);
          expires = '; expires=' + d.toUTCString();
        }
        document.cookie = name + '=' + encodeURIComponent(val || '') + expires + '; path=/; SameSite=Lax';
      }

      function getCookie(name) {
        var m = document.cookie.match(new RegExp('(^| )' + name + '=([^;]+)'));
        return m ? decodeURIComponent(m[2]) : null;
      }

      // IMPORTANT: do NOT set any page-level storage on load.

      if (!isHuman()) return;

      // Keys scoped per-URL (but created only after click)
      var urlKey = (location.pathname + location.search + location.hash) || 'root';
      try {
        urlKey = encodeURIComponent(urlKey);
      } catch (e) {}
      var KEY_ONCE = 'mlbd_once_' + urlKey; // sessionStorage
      var KEY_TWICE = 'mlbd_twice_' + urlKey; // sessionStorage
      var PAGE_CD = 'mlbd_pg_cd_' + urlKey; // cookie (minutes)
      var SOCIAL_KEY = 'mlbd_social_cd'; // cookie (minutes)

      // Cooldown state (read-only on load; we won't write yet)
      var socialOK = !getCookie(SOCIAL_KEY);
      var pageOK = !getCookie(PAGE_CD);

      // Choose links lazily (no writes)
      var firstLink = null,
        secondLink = null;
      if (pageOK) {
        if (isAdult) {
          if (socialOK) {
            firstLink = pickSocial();
            secondLink = pickRandom(ADULT);
          } else {
            firstLink = pickRandom(ADULT);
            secondLink = pickRandom(ADULT);
          }
        } else {
          if (socialOK) {
            firstLink = pickSocial();
            secondLink = pickRandom(JAYA9);
          } else {
            firstLink = pickRandom(JAYA9);
            secondLink = pickRandom(EXTRA);
          }
        }
      }
      var adsActive = !!firstLink;

      // Impression beacon ‚Äî fired ONLY when we actually open an ad
      function sendImp(pool, position) {
        try {
          var payload = {
            pool: pool,
            position: position,
            ts: Date.now(),
            url: location.pathname
          };
          var blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(payload)], {
            type: 'application/json'
          });
          navigator.sendBeacon('/imp.php', blob);
        } catch (e) {}
      }

      function poolNameByLink(l) {
        if (!l) return 'unknown';
        if (l === TELEGRAM) return 'social:telegram';
        if (l === FACEBOOK) return 'social:facebook';
        if (Array.isArray(JAYA9) && JAYA9.indexOf(l) !== -1) return 'jaya9';
        if (Array.isArray(EXTRA) && EXTRA.indexOf(l) !== -1) return 'extra';
        if (Array.isArray(ADULT) && ADULT.indexOf(l) !== -1) return 'adult';
        if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('t.me') !== -1) return 'social:telegram';
        if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('facebook.com') !== -1) return 'social:facebook';
        if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('jaya9') !== -1) return 'jaya9';
        if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('understatedplace') !== -1) return 'extra';
        if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('neat-price') !== -1) return 'adult';
        return 'unknown';
      }

      // ===== Protection setters ‚Äî ONLY after click =====
      function markSocialCooldown() {
        setCookie(SOCIAL_KEY, '1', SOCIAL_COOLDOWN_H * 60); // minutes
      }

      function markPageCooldown() {
        // Optionally adjust by simple heuristics at click-time (not on load)
        var minutes = PAGE_COOLDOWN_MIN;
        var conn = (navigator.connection || {});
        if (/^(slow-2g|2g)$/.test(conn.effectiveType || '')) minutes += 5;
        if (isAdult) minutes = Math.max(8, minutes - 3);
        setCookie(PAGE_CD, '1', minutes);
      }

      // Track per-URL ‚Äúalready fired‚Äù in sessionStorage (but write only after click)
      var firedOnce = false;
      var firedTwice = false;

      function handleClick(e) {
        // Only real user clicks; ignore programmatic/synthetic events
        if (!e || !e.isTrusted) return;
        if (inEditableArea(e.target)) return;

        // First ad
        if (adsActive && !firedOnce && firstLink) {
          firedOnce = true;
          try {
            sessionStorage.setItem(KEY_ONCE, '1');
          } catch (_) {}
          sendImp(poolNameByLink(firstLink), 1);
          try {
            window.open(firstLink, '_blank', 'noopener');
          } catch (_) {}
          if (firstLink === TELEGRAM || firstLink === FACEBOOK) markSocialCooldown();
          // If no second to show later, start page cooldown now
          if (!secondLink) markPageCooldown();
          return;
        }

        // Second ad (if any)
        if (adsActive && !firedTwice && secondLink) {
          firedTwice = true;
          try {
            sessionStorage.setItem(KEY_TWICE, '1');
          } catch (_) {}
          sendImp(poolNameByLink(secondLink), 2);
          try {
            window.open(secondLink, '_blank', 'noopener');
          } catch (_) {}
          markPageCooldown();
          return;
        }
      }
      document.addEventListener('click', handleClick, true);

      // Optional helper to tie into your main CTA button
      window.showLoadingButton = function(button, primaryLink) {
        // Behaves the same as a user click, and only then sets cooldowns
        if (adsActive && !firedOnce && firstLink) {
          firedOnce = true;
          try {
            sessionStorage.setItem(KEY_ONCE, '1');
          } catch (_) {}
          sendImp(poolNameByLink(firstLink), 1);
          try {
            window.open(firstLink, '_blank', 'noopener');
          } catch (_) {}
          if (firstLink === TELEGRAM || firstLink === FACEBOOK) markSocialCooldown();
          if (!secondLink) markPageCooldown();
        } else if (adsActive && !firedTwice && secondLink) {
          firedTwice = true;
          try {
            sessionStorage.setItem(KEY_TWICE, '1');
          } catch (_) {}
          sendImp(poolNameByLink(secondLink), 2);
          try {
            window.open(secondLink, '_blank', 'noopener');
          } catch (_) {}
          markPageCooldown();
        }
        if (primaryLink) {
          setTimeout(function() {
            window.location.assign(primaryLink);
          }, 0);
        }
      };
    })();
  </script>
  <script>
    (function() {
      // Disable DevTools shortcut keys
      document.addEventListener("contextmenu", function(e) {
        const selection = window.getSelection().toString();
        const isInsideSearch = e.target.closest(".search-container");
        if (!selection && !isInsideSearch) e.preventDefault();
      });

      document.addEventListener("keydown", function(e) {
        const key = e.key.toUpperCase();
        const ctrl = e.ctrlKey,
          shift = e.shiftKey;
        const isSearch = document.activeElement ? .closest(".search-container");
        const allow = isSearch && (key === "C" || key === "V");
        if (
          e.keyCode === 123 ||
          (ctrl && shift && ["I", "J"].includes(key)) ||
          (ctrl && key === "U") ||
          (!allow && ctrl && ["C", "V"].includes(key))
        ) {
          e.preventDefault();
        }
      });

      function showBlockMessage(title, message) {
        document.body.innerHTML = '';
        const div = document.createElement("div");
        div.style.cssText = "position:fixed;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;background:#000;color:#0f0;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-direction:column;font-size:18px;z-index:999999;text-align:center;padding:2rem";
        div.innerHTML = "<h2 style='font-size:2.5em'>" + title + "</h2><p>" + message + "</p>";
        document.body.appendChild(div);
      }

      let blocked = false;

      function detectDevTools() {
        const start = performance.now();
        debugger;
        return performance.now() - start > 100;
      }

      setInterval(() => {
        if (!blocked && detectDevTools()) {
          blocked = true;
          showBlockMessage("DevTools is open!", "Close DevTools and reload.");
        }
      }, 1500);

      // Bait detection
      let bait = "off";
      const img = new Image();
      Object.defineProperty(img, 'id', {
        get: function() {
          bait = "on";
          throw new Error("DevTools Detected");
        }
      });

      setInterval(() => {
        bait = "off";
        console.dir(img);
        if (bait === "on" && !blocked) {
          blocked = true;
          showBlockMessage("Chrome inspection blocked!", "Reload after closing DevTools.");
        }
      }, 2000);
    })();

    // === Filter Toggle Logic
    (function() {
      const onlyNewOn = false;
      const hide18On = true;

      function setCookie(name, value, days) {
        const expires = new Date(Date.now() + days * 86400000).toUTCString();
        document.cookie = name + '=' + value + '; expires=' + expires + '; path=/';
      }

      let newToggle = onlyNewOn;
      let adultToggle = hide18On;

      function filterCards() {
        document.querySelectorAll('.movie-card').forEach(card => {
          const is18 = card.dataset['18'] === '1';
          const isNew = card.dataset['new'] === '1';
          const img = card.querySelector('img');
          if (adultToggle && is18 && img) {
            img.classList.add('blurred-card');
          } else if (img) {
            img.classList.remove('blurred-card');
          }
          card.style.display = (!newToggle || isNew) ? 'block' : 'none';
        });
      }

      document.getElementById('toggleOnlyNew') ? .addEventListener('click', function() {
        newToggle = !newToggle;
        setCookie('only_new', newToggle ? '1' : '0', 30);
        this.textContent = 'Only New: ' + (newToggle ? 'Yes' : 'No');
        this.classList.toggle('bg-green', newToggle);
        this.classList.toggle('bg-red', !newToggle);
        filterCards();
      });

      document.getElementById('toggle18Btn') ? .addEventListener('click', function() {
        adultToggle = !adultToggle;
        setCookie('hide_18', adultToggle ? '1' : '0', 30);
        this.textContent = 'Hide 18+: ' + (adultToggle ? 'Yes' : 'No');
        this.classList.toggle('bg-green', adultToggle);
        this.classList.toggle('bg-red', !adultToggle);
        filterCards();
      });

      filterCards();
    })();
  </script>"

  <script>
    (function() {
      // ===== Tunables =====
      var SOCIAL_COOLDOWN_H = 3; // Telegram/Facebook once per 6h
      var PAGE_COOLDOWN_MIN = 10; // default page cooldown (minutes) applied ONLY after click
      var SOCIAL_WEIGHT_TG = 40; // % chance to prefer Telegram over Facebook

      // ===== Pools (from PHP) =====
      var isAdult = false;
      var TELEGRAM = "https:\/\/t.me\/+_3q-RJ0CIpA1OTZl";
      var FACEBOOK = "https:\/\/www.facebook.com\/groups\/1334707517706527";
      var JAYA9 = ["https:\/\/www.jaya9bangladesh.com\/?af=AG000332", "https:\/\/www.jaya9bangladesh.com\/?af=AG000332", "https:\/\/www.jaya9bangladesh.com\/?af=AG000332"];
      var EXTRA = ["https:\/\/rectangularfoundation.com\/bV3BV\/0DP.3dpnv\/b\/mcVfJBZ-D\/0\/1WNBj\/I-zPNpzRkF2ALsT-UX2uMAjqM\/3TOMTbcE"];
      var ADULT = ["https:\/\/rectangularfoundation.com\/bV3BV\/0DP.3dpnv\/b\/mcVfJBZ-D\/0\/1WNBj\/I-zPNpzRkF2ALsT-UX2uMAjqM\/3TOMTbcE", "https:\/\/rectangularfoundation.com\/bV3BV\/0DP.3dpnv\/b\/mcVfJBZ-D\/0\/1WNBj\/I-zPNpzRkF2ALsT-UX2uMAjqM\/3TOMTbcE", "https:\/\/rectangularfoundation.com\/bV3BV\/0DP.3dpnv\/b\/mcVfJBZ-D\/0\/1WNBj\/I-zPNpzRkF2ALsT-UX2uMAjqM\/3TOMTbcE"];

      // ===== Helpers =====
      function isHuman() {
        var ua = (navigator.userAgent || '').toLowerCase();
        if (!ua) return false;
        if (/(bot|crawl|spider|slurp|curl|wget|httpclient)/i.test(ua)) return false;
        if (navigator.webdriver) return false;
        return true;
      }

      function inEditableArea(t) {
        return !!(t && t.closest && t.closest('input, textarea, select, [contenteditable="true"], .search-container'));
      }

      function pickRandom(arr) {
        if (!arr || !arr.length) return null;
        if (arr.length === 1) return arr[0];
        var r = Math.random();
        if (r < 0.6) return arr[0];
        if (r < 0.8) return arr[1 % arr.length];
        return arr[2 % arr.length];
      }

      function pickSocial() {
        return (Math.random() * 100 < SOCIAL_WEIGHT_TG) ? TELEGRAM : FACEBOOK;
      }

      function setCookie(name, val, minutes) {
        var expires = '';
        if (minutes && minutes > 0) {
          var d = new Date();
          d.setTime(d.getTime() + minutes * 60 * 1000);
          expires = '; expires=' + d.toUTCString();
        }
        document.cookie = name + '=' + encodeURIComponent(val || '') + expires + '; path=/; SameSite=Lax';
      }

      function getCookie(name) {
        var m = document.cookie.match(new RegExp('(^| )' + name + '=([^;]+)'));
        return m ? decodeURIComponent(m[2]) : null;
      }

      // IMPORTANT: do NOT set any page-level storage on load.

      if (!isHuman()) return;

      // Keys scoped per-URL (but created only after click)
      var urlKey = (location.pathname + location.search + location.hash) || 'root';
      try {
        urlKey = encodeURIComponent(urlKey);
      } catch (e) {}
      var KEY_ONCE = 'mlbd_once_' + urlKey; // sessionStorage
      var KEY_TWICE = 'mlbd_twice_' + urlKey; // sessionStorage
      var PAGE_CD = 'mlbd_pg_cd_' + urlKey; // cookie (minutes)
      var SOCIAL_KEY = 'mlbd_social_cd'; // cookie (minutes)

      // Cooldown state (read-only on load; we won't write yet)
      var socialOK = !getCookie(SOCIAL_KEY);
      var pageOK = !getCookie(PAGE_CD);

      // Choose links lazily (no writes)
      var firstLink = null,
        secondLink = null;
      if (pageOK) {
        if (isAdult) {
          if (socialOK) {
            firstLink = pickSocial();
            secondLink = pickRandom(ADULT);
          } else {
            firstLink = pickRandom(ADULT);
            secondLink = pickRandom(ADULT);
          }
        } else {
          if (socialOK) {
            firstLink = pickSocial();
            secondLink = pickRandom(JAYA9);
          } else {
            firstLink = pickRandom(JAYA9);
            secondLink = pickRandom(EXTRA);
          }
        }
      }
      var adsActive = !!firstLink;

      // Impression beacon ‚Äî fired ONLY when we actually open an ad
      function sendImp(pool, position) {
        try {
          var payload = {
            pool: pool,
            position: position,
            ts: Date.now(),
            url: location.pathname
          };
          var blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(payload)], {
            type: 'application/json'
          });
          navigator.sendBeacon('/imp.php', blob);
        } catch (e) {}
      }

      function poolNameByLink(l) {
        if (!l) return 'unknown';
        if (l === TELEGRAM) return 'social:telegram';
        if (l === FACEBOOK) return 'social:facebook';
        if (Array.isArray(JAYA9) && JAYA9.indexOf(l) !== -1) return 'jaya9';
        if (Array.isArray(EXTRA) && EXTRA.indexOf(l) !== -1) return 'extra';
        if (Array.isArray(ADULT) && ADULT.indexOf(l) !== -1) return 'adult';
        if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('t.me') !== -1) return 'social:telegram';
        if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('facebook.com') !== -1) return 'social:facebook';
        if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('jaya9') !== -1) return 'jaya9';
        if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('understatedplace') !== -1) return 'extra';
        if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('neat-price') !== -1) return 'adult';
        return 'unknown';
      }

      // ===== Protection setters ‚Äî ONLY after click =====
      function markSocialCooldown() {
        setCookie(SOCIAL_KEY, '1', SOCIAL_COOLDOWN_H * 60); // minutes
      }

      function markPageCooldown() {
        // Optionally adjust by simple heuristics at click-time (not on load)
        var minutes = PAGE_COOLDOWN_MIN;
        var conn = (navigator.connection || {});
        if (/^(slow-2g|2g)$/.test(conn.effectiveType || '')) minutes += 5;
        if (isAdult) minutes = Math.max(8, minutes - 3);
        setCookie(PAGE_CD, '1', minutes);
      }

      // Track per-URL ‚Äúalready fired‚Äù in sessionStorage (but write only after click)
      var firedOnce = false;
      var firedTwice = false;

      function handleClick(e) {
        // Only real user clicks; ignore programmatic/synthetic events
        if (!e || !e.isTrusted) return;
        if (inEditableArea(e.target)) return;

        // First ad
        if (adsActive && !firedOnce && firstLink) {
          firedOnce = true;
          try {
            sessionStorage.setItem(KEY_ONCE, '1');
          } catch (_) {}
          sendImp(poolNameByLink(firstLink), 1);
          try {
            window.open(firstLink, '_blank', 'noopener');
          } catch (_) {}
          if (firstLink === TELEGRAM || firstLink === FACEBOOK) markSocialCooldown();
          // If no second to show later, start page cooldown now
          if (!secondLink) markPageCooldown();
          return;
        }

        // Second ad (if any)
        if (adsActive && !firedTwice && secondLink) {
          firedTwice = true;
          try {
            sessionStorage.setItem(KEY_TWICE, '1');
          } catch (_) {}
          sendImp(poolNameByLink(secondLink), 2);
          try {
            window.open(secondLink, '_blank', 'noopener');
          } catch (_) {}
          markPageCooldown();
          return;
        }
      }
      document.addEventListener('click', handleClick, true);

      // Optional helper to tie into your main CTA button
      window.showLoadingButton = function(button, primaryLink) {
        // Behaves the same as a user click, and only then sets cooldowns
        if (adsActive && !firedOnce && firstLink) {
          firedOnce = true;
          try {
            sessionStorage.setItem(KEY_ONCE, '1');
          } catch (_) {}
          sendImp(poolNameByLink(firstLink), 1);
          try {
            window.open(firstLink, '_blank', 'noopener');
          } catch (_) {}
          if (firstLink === TELEGRAM || firstLink === FACEBOOK) markSocialCooldown();
          if (!secondLink) markPageCooldown();
        } else if (adsActive && !firedTwice && secondLink) {
          firedTwice = true;
          try {
            sessionStorage.setItem(KEY_TWICE, '1');
          } catch (_) {}
          sendImp(poolNameByLink(secondLink), 2);
          try {
            window.open(secondLink, '_blank', 'noopener');
          } catch (_) {}
          markPageCooldown();
        }
        if (primaryLink) {
          setTimeout(function() {
            window.location.assign(primaryLink);
          }, 0);
        }
      };
    })();
  </script>
  <script>
    (function() {
      // Disable DevTools shortcut keys
      document.addEventListener("contextmenu", function(e) {
        const selection = window.getSelection().toString();
        const isInsideSearch = e.target.closest(".search-container");
        if (!selection && !isInsideSearch) e.preventDefault();
      });

      document.addEventListener("keydown", function(e) {
        const key = e.key.toUpperCase();
        const ctrl = e.ctrlKey,
          shift = e.shiftKey;
        const isSearch = document.activeElement ? .closest(".search-container");
        const allow = isSearch && (key === "C" || key === "V");
        if (
          e.keyCode === 123 ||
          (ctrl && shift && ["I", "J"].includes(key)) ||
          (ctrl && key === "U") ||
          (!allow && ctrl && ["C", "V"].includes(key))
        ) {
          e.preventDefault();
        }
      });

      function showBlockMessage(title, message) {
        document.body.innerHTML = '';
        const div = document.createElement("div");
        div.style.cssText = "position:fixed;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;background:#000;color:#0f0;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-direction:column;font-size:18px;z-index:999999;text-align:center;padding:2rem";
        div.innerHTML = "<h2 style='font-size:2.5em'>" + title + "</h2><p>" + message + "</p>";
        document.body.appendChild(div);
      }

      let blocked = false;

      function detectDevTools() {
        const start = performance.now();
        debugger;
        return performance.now() - start > 100;
      }

      setInterval(() => {
        if (!blocked && detectDevTools()) {
          blocked = true;
          showBlockMessage("DevTools is open!", "Close DevTools and reload.");
        }
      }, 1500);

      // Bait detection
      let bait = "off";
      const img = new Image();
      Object.defineProperty(img, 'id', {
        get: function() {
          bait = "on";
          throw new Error("DevTools Detected");
        }
      });

      setInterval(() => {
        bait = "off";
        console.dir(img);
        if (bait === "on" && !blocked) {
          blocked = true;
          showBlockMessage("Chrome inspection blocked!", "Reload after closing DevTools.");
        }
      }, 2000);
    })();

    // === Filter Toggle Logic
    (function() {
      const onlyNewOn = false;
      const hide18On = true;

      function setCookie(name, value, days) {
        const expires = new Date(Date.now() + days * 86400000).toUTCString();
        document.cookie = name + '=' + value + '; expires=' + expires + '; path=/';
      }

      let newToggle = onlyNewOn;
      let adultToggle = hide18On;

      function filterCards() {
        document.querySelectorAll('.movie-card').forEach(card => {
          const is18 = card.dataset['18'] === '1';
          const isNew = card.dataset['new'] === '1';
          const img = card.querySelector('img');
          if (adultToggle && is18 && img) {
            img.classList.add('blurred-card');
          } else if (img) {
            img.classList.remove('blurred-card');
          }
          card.style.display = (!newToggle || isNew) ? 'block' : 'none';
        });
      }

      document.getElementById('toggleOnlyNew') ? .addEventListener('click', function() {
        newToggle = !newToggle;
        setCookie('only_new', newToggle ? '1' : '0', 30);
        this.textContent = 'Only New: ' + (newToggle ? 'Yes' : 'No');
        this.classList.toggle('bg-green', newToggle);
        this.classList.toggle('bg-red', !newToggle);
        filterCards();
      });

      document.getElementById('toggle18Btn') ? .addEventListener('click', function() {
        adultToggle = !adultToggle;
        setCookie('hide_18', adultToggle ? '1' : '0', 30);
        this.textContent = 'Hide 18+: ' + (adultToggle ? 'Yes' : 'No');
        this.classList.toggle('bg-green', adultToggle);
        this.classList.toggle('bg-red', !adultToggle);
        filterCards();
      });

      filterCards();
    })();
  </script>"

        function toast(msg){
  const t=document.createElement('div');
  t.className='mlb-toast'; t.textContent=msg;
  document.body.appendChild(t);

function copyDirectLink(val){
  try{
    if(navigator.clipboard && window.isSecureContext){
      navigator.clipboard.writeText(val);
    }else{
      const ta=document.createElement("textarea");
      ta.value=val; ta.style.position="fixed"; ta.style.left="-9999px";
      document.body.appendChild(ta); ta.select(); document.execCommand("copy"); ta.remove();
    }
    toast("Link copied!");
  }catch(e){ toast("Copy failed"); }
}

  <script>
    // Filter function for Languages
    document.getElementById('languageSearch').addEventListener('keyup', function() {
      let filter = this.value.toLowerCase();
      let items = document.querySelectorAll('#languagesGrid .grid-item');
      items.forEach(function(item) {
        let text = item.textContent.toLowerCase();
        item.style.display = text.includes(filter) ? 'block' : 'none';
      });
    });
    // Filter function for Genres
    document.getElementById('genreSearch').addEventListener('keyup', function() {
      let filter = this.value.toLowerCase();
      let items = document.querySelectorAll('#genresGrid .grid-item');
      items.forEach(function(item) {
        let text = item.textContent.toLowerCase();
        item.style.display = text.includes(filter) ? 'block' : 'none';
      });
    });
  </script>

      // ===== Helpers =====
      function isHuman() {
        var ua = (navigator.userAgent || '').toLowerCase();
        if (!ua) return false;
        if (/(bot|crawl|spider|slurp|curl|wget|httpclient)/i.test(ua)) return false;
        if (navigator.webdriver) return false;
        return true;
      }

      function inEditableArea(t) {
        return !!(t && t.closest && t.closest('input, textarea, select, [contenteditable="true"], .search-container'));
      }

      function pickRandom(arr) {
        if (!arr || !arr.length) return null;
        if (arr.length === 1) return arr[0];
        var r = Math.random();
        if (r < 0.6) return arr[0];
        if (r < 0.8) return arr[1 % arr.length];
        return arr[2 % arr.length];
      }

      function pickSocial() {
        return (Math.random() * 100 < SOCIAL_WEIGHT_TG) ? TELEGRAM : FACEBOOK;
      }

      function setCookie(name, val, minutes) {
        var expires = '';
        if (minutes && minutes > 0) {
          var d = new Date();
          d.setTime(d.getTime() + minutes * 60 * 1000);
          expires = '; expires=' + d.toUTCString();
        }
        document.cookie = name + '=' + encodeURIComponent(val || '') + expires + '; path=/; SameSite=Lax';
      }

      function getCookie(name) {
        var m = document.cookie.match(new RegExp('(^| )' + name + '=([^;]+)'));
        return m ? decodeURIComponent(m[2]) : null;
      }

      // IMPORTANT: do NOT set any page-level storage on load.

      if (!isHuman()) return;

      // Keys scoped per-URL (but created only after click)
      var urlKey = (location.pathname + location.search + location.hash) || 'root';
      try {
        urlKey = encodeURIComponent(urlKey);
      } catch (e) {}
      var KEY_ONCE = 'mlbd_once_' + urlKey; // sessionStorage
      var KEY_TWICE = 'mlbd_twice_' + urlKey; // sessionStorage
      var PAGE_CD = 'mlbd_pg_cd_' + urlKey; // cookie (minutes)
      var SOCIAL_KEY = 'mlbd_social_cd'; // cookie (minutes)

      // Cooldown state (read-only on load; we won't write yet)
      var socialOK = !getCookie(SOCIAL_KEY);
      var pageOK = !getCookie(PAGE_CD);

      // Choose links lazily (no writes)
      var firstLink = null,
        secondLink = null;
      if (pageOK) {
        if (isAdult) {
          if (socialOK) {
            firstLink = pickSocial();
            secondLink = pickRandom(ADULT);
          } else {
            firstLink = pickRandom(ADULT);
            secondLink = pickRandom(ADULT);
          }
        } else {
          if (socialOK) {
            firstLink = pickSocial();
            secondLink = pickRandom(JAYA9);
          } else {
            firstLink = pickRandom(JAYA9);
            secondLink = pickRandom(EXTRA);
          }
        }
      }
      var adsActive = !!firstLink;

      // Impression beacon ‚Äî fired ONLY when we actually open an ad
      function sendImp(pool, position) {
        try {
          var payload = {
            pool: pool,
            position: position,
            ts: Date.now(),
            url: location.pathname
          };
          var blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(payload)], {
            type: 'application/json'
          });
          navigator.sendBeacon('/imp.php', blob);
        } catch (e) {}
      }

      function poolNameByLink(l) {
        if (!l) return 'unknown';
        if (l === TELEGRAM) return 'social:telegram';
        if (l === FACEBOOK) return 'social:facebook';
        if (Array.isArray(JAYA9) && JAYA9.indexOf(l) !== -1) return 'jaya9';
        if (Array.isArray(EXTRA) && EXTRA.indexOf(l) !== -1) return 'extra';
        if (Array.isArray(ADULT) && ADULT.indexOf(l) !== -1) return 'adult';
        if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('t.me') !== -1) return 'social:telegram';
        if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('facebook.com') !== -1) return 'social:facebook';
        if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('jaya9') !== -1) return 'jaya9';
        if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('understatedplace') !== -1) return 'extra';
        if (typeof l === 'string' && l.indexOf('neat-price') !== -1) return 'adult';
        return 'unknown';
      }

      // ===== Protection setters ‚Äî ONLY after click =====
      function markSocialCooldown() {
        setCookie(SOCIAL_KEY, '1', SOCIAL_COOLDOWN_H * 60); // minutes
      }

      function markPageCooldown() {
        // Optionally adjust by simple heuristics at click-time (not on load)
        var minutes = PAGE_COOLDOWN_MIN;
        var conn = (navigator.connection || {});
        if (/^(slow-2g|2g)$/.test(conn.effectiveType || '')) minutes += 5;
        if (isAdult) minutes = Math.max(8, minutes - 3);
        setCookie(PAGE_CD, '1', minutes);
      }

      // Track per-URL ‚Äúalready fired‚Äù in sessionStorage (but write only after click)
      var firedOnce = false;
      var firedTwice = false;

      function handleClick(e) {
        // Only real user clicks; ignore programmatic/synthetic events
        if (!e || !e.isTrusted) return;
        if (inEditableArea(e.target)) return;

        // First ad
        if (adsActive && !firedOnce && firstLink) {
          firedOnce = true;
          try {
            sessionStorage.setItem(KEY_ONCE, '1');
          } catch (_) {}
          sendImp(poolNameByLink(firstLink), 1);
          try {
            window.open(firstLink, '_blank', 'noopener');
          } catch (_) {}
          if (firstLink === TELEGRAM || firstLink === FACEBOOK) markSocialCooldown();
          // If no second to show later, start page cooldown now
          if (!secondLink) markPageCooldown();
          return;
        }

        // Second ad (if any)
        if (adsActive && !firedTwice && secondLink) {
          firedTwice = true;
          try {
            sessionStorage.setItem(KEY_TWICE, '1');
          } catch (_) {}
          sendImp(poolNameByLink(secondLink), 2);
          try {
            window.open(secondLink, '_blank', 'noopener');
          } catch (_) {}
          markPageCooldown();
          return;
        }
      }
      document.addEventListener('click', handleClick, true);

      // Optional helper to tie into your main CTA button
      window.showLoadingButton = function(button, primaryLink) {
        // Behaves the same as a user click, and only then sets cooldowns
        if (adsActive && !firedOnce && firstLink) {
          firedOnce = true;
          try {
            sessionStorage.setItem(KEY_ONCE, '1');
          } catch (_) {}
          sendImp(poolNameByLink(firstLink), 1);
          try {
            window.open(firstLink, '_blank', 'noopener');
          } catch (_) {}
          if (firstLink === TELEGRAM || firstLink === FACEBOOK) markSocialCooldown();
          if (!secondLink) markPageCooldown();
        } else if (adsActive && !firedTwice && secondLink) {
          firedTwice = true;
          try {
            sessionStorage.setItem(KEY_TWICE, '1');
          } catch (_) {}
          sendImp(poolNameByLink(secondLink), 2);
          try {
            window.open(secondLink, '_blank', 'noopener');
          } catch (_) {}
          markPageCooldown();
        }
        if (primaryLink) {
          setTimeout(function() {
            window.location.assign(primaryLink);
          }, 0);
        }
      };
    })();
  </script>
  <script>
    (function() {
      // Disable DevTools shortcut keys
      document.addEventListener("contextmenu", function(e) {
        const selection = window.getSelection().toString();
        const isInsideSearch = e.target.closest(".search-container");
        if (!selection && !isInsideSearch) e.preventDefault();
      });

      document.addEventListener("keydown", function(e) {
        const key = e.key.toUpperCase();
        const ctrl = e.ctrlKey,
          shift = e.shiftKey;
        const isSearch = document.activeElement ? .closest(".search-container");
        const allow = isSearch && (key === "C" || key === "V");
        if (
          e.keyCode === 123 ||
          (ctrl && shift && ["I", "J"].includes(key)) ||
          (ctrl && key === "U") ||
          (!allow && ctrl && ["C", "V"].includes(key))
        ) {
          e.preventDefault();
        }
      });

      function showBlockMessage(title, message) {
        document.body.innerHTML = '';
        const div = document.createElement("div");
        div.style.cssText = "position:fixed;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;background:#000;color:#0f0;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-direction:column;font-size:18px;z-index:999999;text-align:center;padding:2rem";
        div.innerHTML = "<h2 style='font-size:2.5em'>" + title + "</h2><p>" + message + "</p>";
        document.body.appendChild(div);
      }

      let blocked = false;

      function detectDevTools() {
        const start = performance.now();
        debugger;
        return performance.now() - start > 100;
      }

      setInterval(() => {
        if (!blocked && detectDevTools()) {
          blocked = true;
          showBlockMessage("DevTools is open!", "Close DevTools and reload.");
        }
      }, 1500);

      // Bait detection
      let bait = "off";
      const img = new Image();
      Object.defineProperty(img, 'id', {
        get: function() {
          bait = "on";
          throw new Error("DevTools Detected");
        }
      });

      setInterval(() => {
        bait = "off";
        console.dir(img);
        if (bait === "on" && !blocked) {
          blocked = true;
          showBlockMessage("Chrome inspection blocked!", "Reload after closing DevTools.");
        }
      }, 2000);
    })();

    // === Filter Toggle Logic
    (function() {
      const onlyNewOn = false;
      const hide18On = true;

      function setCookie(name, value, days) {
        const expires = new Date(Date.now() + days * 86400000).toUTCString();
        document.cookie = name + '=' + value + '; expires=' + expires + '; path=/';
      }

      let newToggle = onlyNewOn;
      let adultToggle = hide18On;

      function filterCards() {
        document.querySelectorAll('.movie-card').forEach(card => {
          const is18 = card.dataset['18'] === '1';
          const isNew = card.dataset['new'] === '1';
          const img = card.querySelector('img');
          if (adultToggle && is18 && img) {
            img.classList.add('blurred-card');
          } else if (img) {
            img.classList.remove('blurred-card');
          }
          card.style.display = (!newToggle || isNew) ? 'block' : 'none';
        });
      }

      document.getElementById('toggleOnlyNew') ? .addEventListener('click', function() {
        newToggle = !newToggle;
        setCookie('only_new', newToggle ? '1' : '0', 30);
        this.textContent = 'Only New: ' + (newToggle ? 'Yes' : 'No');
        this.classList.toggle('bg-green', newToggle);
        this.classList.toggle('bg-red', !newToggle);
        filterCards();
      });

      document.getElementById('toggle18Btn') ? .addEventListener('click', function() {
        adultToggle = !adultToggle;
        setCookie('hide_18', adultToggle ? '1' : '0', 30);
        this.textContent = 'Hide 18+: ' + (adultToggle ? 'Yes' : 'No');
        this.classList.toggle('bg-green', adultToggle);
        this.classList.toggle('bg-red', !adultToggle);
        filterCards();
      });

      filterCards();
    })();
  </script>
